Или наоборот.									ノーツとのタイミングが <b>遅い</b> 場合、数値を <b>増やして</b> 下さい。また、逆も同様です。	如果你觉得 Note 比音乐要<b>早</b>，请<b>增加</b>偏移；\n否则，请减少偏移。	譜面<b>太快</b>就<b>增加</b>數值；譜面<b>太慢</b>則<b>減少</b>數值。\n以 0.01 秒（方框）／0.05 秒（圓框）為單位\n左右增減來進行調整。	노트가 노래보다 <b>더 빠르게<b> 나온다고 생각하시면, 소리 오프셋 값을 <b>추가<b> 해주세요.	Pokud cítíte, že noty jsou <b>napřed</b> před hudbou, <b>zvyšte</b> offset. To samé obráceně.								Nếu bạn cảm thấy nốt đang <b> trước</b> nhạc thì <b> tăng </b> mức bù thời gian và ngược lại. STORY_TRAINING_15		Simply put,^ the level system calculates a †"RT Score"† for each of your uploaded records.^^/Two factors affect this score: †level difficulty† and †accuracy†.					Resumindo,^ o sistema de níveis calcula uma †"Pontuação RT"† para cada performance enviada..^^/Dois fatores afetam essa pontuação: †dificuldade do nível† e †precisão†.												简单来说，^对于每条上传到 Cytoid 的游玩记录，^^/系统都会计算出这条记录对应的†分值†。^^/†关卡的难度等级与你的精确度会决定分值的高低。†	簡單來說，^對於每條上傳到 Cytoid 的遊玩記錄，^^/系統都會計算出這條記錄對應的†分值†。 ^^/†關卡的難度等級與你的精確度會決定分值的高低。 †		Jednoduše řečeno,^ systém hodnocení počítá †"RT skóre"† pro každý nahraný rekord.^^/Dva faktory ovlivňují toto skóre: †obtížnost úrovně† a †tvoje přesnost†.								Nói đơn giản, hệ thống này được tính bởi một †"RT Score"† cho mỗi kết quả ghi nhận được.^^Có 2 yếu tố là †độ khó của level† và †độ chính xác†				
STORY_TRAINING_16		For example,^ if you achieve 100% accuracy on a Lv.3 level,^ then the RT score is 3 × 100% = 3.00.^^ If you achieve 97% accuracy on a Lv.15 level,^ then the RT score is 15 × 97% = 14.55.					Por exemplo,^ Se você conseguir 100% de precisão em um nível de dificuldade 3,^ então a pontuação RT será de 3 × 100% = 3.00.^^ Se você alcançar uma precisão de 97% em um nível de dificuldade 15,^ então a pontuação RT será 15 × 97% = 14.55.												举例的话，^^/在 Lv.3 的关卡取得 100% 精确度，^分值就是 3 × 100% = 3.00。^^/在 Lv.15 的关卡取得 97% 精确度，^分值就是 15 × 97% = 14.55。	舉例的話，^^/在 Lv.3 的關卡取得 100% 精確度，^分值就是 3 × 100% = 3.00。 ^^/在 Lv.15 的關卡取得 97% 精確度，^分值就是 15 × 97% = 14.55。		Na příklad,^ když zahraješ 100% přesnost na úrovni s obtížností 3,^ potom RT skóre je 3 x 100% = 3.00.^^ Když zahraješ 97% přesnost na úrovni s obtížností 15,^ potom RT skóre je 15 x 97% = 14.55.								Ví dụ,^ nếu bạn đạt 100% độ chính xác ở một level Lv.3, thì RT Score là 3 × 100% = 3.00.^^ Tương tự nếu bạn đạt được 97% độ chính xác ở một level có Lv.15 thì RT Score là 15 × 97% = 14.55.

Do NOT translate!	<size=48><b>Copyright Policy</b></size>\n\n\nCytoid is a noncommercial and player-driven game. <b>We do not generate any profit, either directly or indirectly, and our operation relies entirely on user donations.</b> As outlined in our terms of services, all game levels are created and uploaded by community members, and although we always ask them to obtain permissions from and provide attributions to relevant copyright holders, it may not be observed in some cases.\n\nWe respect the intellectual property rights of others just as we expect others to respect our rights. If you believe that content residing on or accessible through Cytoid's services infringes your copyright, pursuant to Digital Millennium Copyright Act, Title 17, United States Code, Section 512(c), a copyright owner or their agent may submit a takedown notice to us via our DMCA Agent listed below. As an internet service provider, we are entitled to claim immunity from said infringement claims pursuant to the “safe harbor” provisions of the DMCA. To submit a good faith infringement claim to us, you must submit notice to us that sets forth the following information:\n\n<size=36>Notice of Infringement – Claim</size>\n\n1. A physical or electronic signature of the copyright owner (or someone authorized to act on behalf of the owner);\n2. Identification of the copyrighted work claimed to have been infringed;\n3. Identification of the infringing material to be removed, and information reasonably sufficient to permit the service provider to locate the material;\n4. Information reasonably sufficient to permit the service provider to contact the complaining party including your name, physical address, email address, phone number and fax number;\n5. A statement that the complaining party has a good faith belief that the use of the material is unauthorized by the copyright agent; and\n6. A statement that the information in the notification is accurate, and, under penalty of perjury, that the complaining party is authorized to act on behalf of the copyright owner.\n\nTitle 17 USC §512(f) provides civil damage penalties, including costs and attorney fees, against any person who knowingly and materially misrepresents certain information in a notification of infringement under 17 USC §512(c)(3).\n\nPlease note that we may share the identity and information in any copyright infringement claim we receive with the alleged infringer. In submitting a claim, you understand accept and agree that your identity and claim may be communicated to the alleged infringer.\n\nSend all takedown notices to our DMCA Agent, whose contact is listed below.\n\n<size=36>Counter Notification - Restoration of Material</size>\n\nIf you have received a notice of material being takedown because of a copyright infringement claim, you may provide us with a counter notification in an effort to have the material in question restored to the site. Said notification must be given in writing to our DMCA Agent and must contain substantially the following elements pursuant to 17 USC Section 512(g)(3):\n\n1. Your physical or electronic signature.\n2. A description of the material that has been taken down and the original location of the material before it was taken down.\n3. A statement under penalty of perjury that you have a good faith belief that the material was removed or disabled as a result of mistake or misidentification of the material to be removed or disabled.\n4. Your name, address, and telephone number, and a statement that you consent to the jurisdiction of the federal district court for the judicial district in which the address is located (or if you are outside of the United States, that you consent to jurisdiction of any judicial district in which the service provider may be found), and that the you will accept service of process from the person or company who provided the original infringement notification.\n\nEmail your counter notice to our DMCA Agent, whose contact is listed below.\n\n<size=36>Repeat Infringer Policy</size>\n\nWe take copyright infringement very seriously. Pursuant to the repeat infringer policy requirements of the Digital Millennium Copyright Act, we maintain a list of DMCA notices from copyright holders and make a good faith effort to identify any repeat infringers. Those that violate our internal repeat infringer policy will have their accounts terminated.\n\n<size=36>Designated Agent Contact</size>\n\nEmail: dmca@cytoid.io\n\nPostal address:\n\n    DMCA Agent   \n    400 Mccutcheon Dr  \n    West Lafayette, IN 47906\n\n<size=36>Attribution</size>\n\nPart of this text is based on "osu! copyright policy" (https://github.com/ppy/osu-wiki/blob/master/wiki/Legal/Copyright/en.md), licensed under CC-BY-NC 4.0.																	<size=48><b>版权政策</b></size>\n\n\nCytoid 是一款非商业性的、由社区驱动的游戏。<b>我们不直接或间接地产生任何利润；事实上，我们没有任何形式的盈利手段（包括广告），运营完全依赖于用户的捐赠。</b>正如我们的服务条款中所概述的那样，所有的游戏关卡都是由社区成员创建和上传的，尽管我们总是要求他们获得相关版权所有者的许可并提供归属，但在某些情况下这可能不会被遵守。\n\n我们尊重他人的知识产权，正如我们希望他人尊重我们的权利。如果您认为托管在 Cytoid 服务上或任何通过 Cytoid 服务访问到的内容侵犯了您的版权，根据《美国法典》第 17 章数字千年版权法案第 512(c) 条，版权所有者或其代理人可以通过我们的 DMCA 代理向我们提交移除通知。作为互联网服务提供商，根据 DMCA 的「安全港」条款，我们依法享有条款中的豁免权，使我们免受版权主张所致之责任。要向我们提交忠实的版权主张，您必须向我们提交包含以下信息的通知。\n\n<size=36>侵权通知（版权主张）</size>\n\n1. 著作权人（或授权代表著作权人的人）的纸质或电子签名；\n2. 声称被侵权的版权作品的标识；\n3. 需要删除的侵权材料的标识，以及足以让服务提供商找到该材料的合理信息；\n4. 足以让服务提供商联系投诉方的合理信息，包括您的姓名、物理地址、电子邮件地址、电话号码和传真号码；\n5. 一份声明，说明投诉方有充分的理由相信该材料的使用是未经版权代理授权的；\n6. 声明通知中的信息是准确的，并在作伪证的惩罚下，声明投诉方被授权代表版权所有者行事。\n\n《美国法典》第 17 章第 512(f) 条规定，任何人如果根据《美国法典》第 17 章第 512(c)(3) 条在侵权通知中故意并在实质上歪曲某些信息，将受到民事损害处罚，包括费用和律师费。\n\n请注意，我们可能会与被控侵权者分享我们收到的任何版权版权主张中的身份和信息。在提交版权主张时，您理解并同意您的身份和版权主张可能会被告知被指控的侵权者。\n\n请将所有移除通知发送给我们的 DMCA 代理，其联系方式于文末。\n\n<size=36>抗辩通知（内容恢复）</size>\n\n如果您收到了由于版权版权主张而被撤下的材料通知，您可以向我们提供一份抗辩通知，以努力使有关材料恢复到网站上。上述通知必须以书面形式发给我们的 DMCA 代理，并且必须根据《美国联邦法典》第 17 章第 512(g)(3) 条的规定包含以下内容。\n\n1. 您的纸质或电子签名。\n2. 对被撤下的材料的描述，以及材料被撤下前的原始位置。\n3. 在伪证罪的惩罚下，声明您有诚意相信该材料是由于错误或误认要删除或禁用的材料而被删除或禁用的。\n4. 您的姓名、地址和电话号码，以及一份声明，表明您同意接受地址所在司法区的联邦地区法院的管辖（或者如果您在美国境外，您同意接受服务提供者所在的任何司法区的管辖），并且您将接受提供原始侵权通知的个人或公司的送达。\n\n请将您的抗辩通知通过电子邮件发送给我们的 DMCA 代理，其联系方式于文末。\n\n<size=36>反复侵权者政策</size>\n\n我们非常严肃地对待版权侵权行为。根据《数字千年版权法》对反复侵权者的政策要求，我们保留了一份来自版权持有人的 DMCA 通知清单，并努力识别任何反复侵权者。违反我们内部反复侵权者政策的人，其账户将被终止。\n\n<size=36>指定代理人联系方式</size>\n\n邮件地址：dmca@cytoid.io\n\n通讯地址：\n\n    DMCA Agent   \n    400 Mccutcheon Dr  \n    West Lafayette, IN 47906\n\n<size=36>归属</size>\n\n原文部分内容基于「osu! 版权政策」，根据 CC-BY-NC 4.0 许可获得授权。	<size=48><b>版權政策</b></size>\n\n\nCytoid 是一款非商業性的、由社群協力運作的遊戲。 <b>我們不直接或間接地產生任何利潤；事實上，我們沒有任何形式的盈利手段（包括廣告），營運完全依賴於使用者的捐贈。 </b>正如我們的服務條款中所概述的那樣，所有的遊戲關卡都是由社群成員創建和上傳的，儘管我們總是要求他們獲得相關版權所有者的許可並提供歸屬，但在某些情況下這可能不會被遵守。 \n\n我們尊重他人的智慧財產權，正如我們希望他人尊重我們的權利。如果您認為託管在 Cytoid 服務上或任何透過 Cytoid 服務存取到的內容侵犯了您的版權，根據《美國法典》第 17 章數字千年版權法案第 512(c) 條，版權所有者或其代理人可以通過我們的 DMCA 代理向我們提交移除通知。作為網際網路服務供應商，根據 DMCA 的「安全港」條款，我們依法享有條款中的豁免權，使我們免受版權主張所致之責任。 要向我們提交忠實的版權主張，您必須向我們提交包含以下資訊的通知。 \n\n<size=36>侵權通知（版權主張）</size>\n\n1. 著作權人（或授權代表著作權人的人）的紙本或電子簽名；\n2. 聲稱被侵權的版權作品的標誌；\n3. 需要刪除的侵權材料的標誌，以及足以讓服務供應商找到該材料的合理資訊；\n4. 足以讓服務供應商聯繫投訴方的合理資訊，包括您的姓名、物理地址、電子郵件地址、電話號碼和傳真號碼；\n5. 一份聲明，說明投訴方有充分的理由相信該材料的使用是未經版權代理授權的；\n6. 聲明通知中的資訊是準確的，並在作偽證的懲罰下，聲明投訴方被授權代表版權所有者行事。 \n\n《美國法典》第17 章第 512(f) 條規定，任何人如果根據《美國法典》第17 章第 512(c)(3) 條在侵權通知中故意並在實質上歪曲某些資訊，將受到民事損害處罰，包括費用和律師費。 \n\n請注意，我們可能會與被控侵權者分享我們收到的任何版權版權主張中的身份和資訊。在提交版權主張時，您理解並同意您的身份和版權主張可能會被告知被指控的侵權者。 \n\n請將所有移除通知發送給我們的 DMCA 代理，其聯繫方式於文末。 \n\n<size=36>抗辯通知（內容恢復）</size>\n\n如果您收到了由於版權版權主張而被撤下的材料通知，您可以向我們提供一份抗辯通知，以努力使有關材料恢復到網站上。上述通知必須以書面形式發給我們的 DMCA 代理，並且必須根據《美國聯邦法典》第 17 章第 512(g)(3) 條的規定包含以下內容。 \n\n1. 您的紙本或電子簽名。 \n2. 對被撤下的材料的描述，以及材料被撤下前的原始位置。 \n3. 在偽證罪的懲罰下，聲明您有誠意相信該材料是由於錯誤或誤認要刪除或禁用的材料而被刪除或禁用的。 \n4. 您的姓名、地址和電話號碼，以及一份聲明，表明您同意接受地址所在司法區的聯邦地區法院的管轄（或者如果您在美國境外，您同意接受服務提供者所在的任何司法區的管轄），並且您將接受提供原始侵權通知的個人或公司的送達。 \n\n請將您的抗辯通知通過電子郵件發送給我們的 DMCA 代理，其聯繫方式於文末。 \n\n<size=36>反覆侵權者政策</size>\n\n我們非常嚴肅地對待版權侵權行為。根據《數字千年版權法》對反覆侵權者的政策要求，我們保留了一份來自版權持有人的 DMCA 通知清單，並努力辨識任何反覆侵權者。違反我們內部反覆侵權者政策的人，其帳戶將被終止。 \n\n<size=36>指定代理人聯繫方式</size>\n\n郵件地址：dmca@cytoid.io\n\n通訊地址：\n\n    DMCA Agent \n    400 Mccutcheon Dr \n    West Lafayette, IN 47906\n\n<size=36>歸屬</size>\n\n原文部分內容基於「osu! 版權政策」，根據 CC-BY-NC 4.0 許可獲得授權。
